இப்ெபாᾨᾐம்கூட அரசாங்கம் விᾞம்பினால், ஜனாதிபதி விᾞம்பினால், சுதந்திரத்திற்குப் பிறகு அᾌத்தᾌத்ᾐ வந்த அத்தைன அரசாங்கங்களினᾐம் ெதாடர்ச்சியான இனெவறிக் ெகாள்ைககளின் விைளவாக இன்ைறக்கு எாிந்ᾐ ெகாண்ᾊᾞக்கின்ற இந்த இலங்ைகத் தீவின் இனப் பிரச்சிைனக்கு, ேதசியக் ேகள்விக்கு சமாதான வழியில் அரசியல் ாீதியாகத் தீர்ᾫ காண ᾙᾊᾜம். அதற்கு இன்னᾙம் காலம் கடந்ᾐவிடவில்ைல. ஆனால், அரசாங்கத்தின் ேநாக்கம் அᾐவல்ல! சாதாரண சிங்கள மக்கைள ஏமாற்றி, ᾜத்த ெவறிைய ஊட்ᾊ, ᾗᾢகள்வசம் எஞ்சியிᾞக்கின்ற குᾠகிய பிரேதசத்ைதᾜம் ைகப்பற்றி, ஏேதா, தமிழ் இனத்தின் ேதசிய எᾨச்சிைய நிரந்தரமாக அடக்கிவிட்ேடாம் என்ற நிைனப்ைபச் சிங்கள மக்கᾦக்கு ஊட்ᾌவதன்ᾚலம் தமᾐ பதவிையத் ெதாடர்ந்ᾐம் நீᾊக்கᾙᾊᾜம் என இந்த அரசாங்கம் நம்ᾗகிறᾐ. இந்த ᾜத்தெவறிைய ஊட்ᾌவதன்ᾚலம் சாதாரண சிங்கள மக்கள் மத்தியிேல ஏற்பட்ᾌள்ள சிந்தைனப்ேபாக்கு அதிக காலம் நீᾊக்காᾐ என்பைத மட்ᾌம் நான் ெசால்ᾢக்ெகாள்ள

விᾞம்ᾗகின்ேறன். இந்த ᾜத்தம் ᾙᾊᾫக்கு வந்ததன் பின்னர் சாதாரண சிங்கள மக்கள் தமᾐ அன்றாட வாழ்க்ைகையப் பாதிக்கின்ற ெபாᾞளாதாரப் பிரச்சிைனையப் பற்றிச் சிந்திக்க ᾙற்பᾌவார்கள். அᾐதான் அவர்கᾦைடய அᾊப்பைடப் பிரச்சிைனயாக இᾞக்கும். ஆகேவ, இந்த அரசாங்கம் தயᾫெசய்ᾐ தப்ᾗக்கணக்குப் ேபாடக்கூடாᾐ.

ஒன்ᾠபட்ட நாட்ᾌக்குள்ேள இந்தப் பிரச்சிைனையத் தீர்க்க விᾞம்பினால் எங்கிᾞந்ᾐ எத்தைகய எதிர்ப்ᾗ வந்தாᾤம் தனᾐ ᾘரணமான ஒத்ᾐைழப்ைப வழங்குெமன தமிழ்த் ேதசியக் கூட்டைமப்ᾗ இப்ெபாᾨᾐம் ெசால்கிறᾐ; நாங்கள் அதைனச் சந்திக்கத் தயாராக இᾞக்கிேறாம். ஒᾞ காலத்தில் தமிழீழ விᾌதைலப் ᾗᾢகளின் ெகாைலப்பட்ᾊயᾢல்கூட எங்களில் பலர் இᾞந்திᾞக்கிேறாம். நாங்கள் மரணத்ைதக் கண்ᾌ அஞ்சியᾐம் இல்ைல; அஞ்சப்ேபாவᾐமில்ைல. இப்ெபாᾨᾐம்கூட எங்கᾦக்கு அச்சுᾠத்தல்கள் இᾞக்கின்றன. எங்கᾦைடய பாராᾦமன்ற உᾠப்பினர்கள் பலர் ெகால்லப்பட்ᾊᾞக்கிறார்கள் என்பᾐ எல்ேலாᾞக்கும் ெதாிᾜம். ஆகேவ, எங்கᾦக்கு ஏற்பட்ᾌள்ள இத்தைகய அச்சுᾠத்தல்கᾦக்கு மத்தியிᾤம்கூட, தமிழ்த் ேதசியக் கூட்டைமப்ᾗ தமிழ் மக்கᾦைடய ேதசிய அபிலாைஷகைள ᾙன்ெனᾌப்பதிேல ஒᾞெபாᾨᾐம் விட்ᾌக்ெகாᾌக்கமாட்டாᾐ என்பைத நான் இந்தச் சைபயிேல பிரகடனப்பᾌத்த விᾞம்ᾗகின்ேறன். அேதேநரத்தில், சாதாரண சிங்கள மக்கᾦக்கும் சாதாரண தமிழ்ப் ெபாᾐமக்கᾦக்குமிைடயிேல எந்தப் பிரச்சிைனᾜம் கிைடயாᾐ. பாரம்பாியமிக்க இந்த இரண்ᾌ இனங்கைளᾜம் ேசர்ந்த மக்கள் இனிᾜம்கூட இந்த நாட்ᾊேல அைமதியாக வாழக்கூᾊய சூழ்நிைல இᾞக்கின்றᾐ. ஆனால், அைதக் ெகᾌத்ᾐக்ெகாண்ᾊᾞப்பᾐ அரசியல்வாதிகள் - பதவி ெவறிபிᾊத்த அரசியல்வாதிகள் - சாதாரண மக்களின் வாக்குகைள ஏமாற்றிப் ெபற்ᾠ, பதவிச் சுகத்திைன அᾌத்தᾌத்ᾐ வந்த அரசாங்கங்களிᾕடாக அᾔபவித்ᾐ வந்திᾞக்கின்ற அரசியல்வாதிகள் என்பᾐ எங்கᾦக்கு நன்றாகத் ெதாிᾜம்! இப்ெபாᾨᾐம்கூட சிங்கள மக்கᾦக்கு ேநசக்கரம் நீட்ᾌவதற்குத் தமிழ் மக்கள் தயாராக இᾞக்கின்றார்கள். அைதப் பற்றிப் பிᾊப்பதற்கு இந்த அரசாங்கம் தயாெரன்றால், சிங்கள மக்களின் சார்பிேல ஜனாதிபதி அவர்கள் தயாெரன்றால், இந்தப் பிரச்சிைனைய ஒன்ᾠபட்ட நாட்ᾌக்குள்ேள தீர்க்க ᾙᾊᾜம். பிரபாகரன்கள் வரலாம், ேபாகலாம்; ெபாட்ᾌ அம்மான்கள் வரலாம், ேபாகலாம்; தமிழ்ச்ெசல்வன்கள் வரலாம், ேபாகலாம். ஆனால், தமிழ்த் ேதசிய எᾨச்சி என்பᾐ, பிரபாகரன் என்ற ெபயைர இந்த நாᾌ அறிவதற்கு ᾙன்னேர இந்த மண்ணில் ஏற்பட்டெதன்பைத மறந்ᾐவிடாதீர்கள்! பிரபாகரைன உᾞவாக்கியᾐ சிங்கள-ெபளத்த இனெவறி என்பைத மறந்ᾐவிடாதீர்கள்! அைதத்தான் நாங்கள் அᾨத்தந்திᾞத்தமாகக் கூறிக்ெகாள்ள விᾞம்ᾗகின்ேறாம். எனேவ, இந்தப் பிரச்சிைன ஏன் ஏற்பட்டᾐ, எதனால் ஏற்பட்டெதன்பைதச் சிந்தித்ᾐ இனியாவᾐ, இப்ெபாᾨᾐதாவᾐ, இந்த அரசாங்கᾙம் ேமதகு ஜனாதிபதி அவர்கᾦம் குᾠகிய அரசியல் சிந்தைனக்கப்பால் சிந்திக்கத் தயாராக இᾞந்தால் ெவளிநாᾌகைளக் குைறெசால்ᾤம் நிைலைம வராᾐ. ெவளிநாட்டவர்கள் ஏன் வᾞகின்றார்கள்? அதற்குக் காரணம் நீங்கள்! இங்ேக ஏற்பட்ᾊᾞக்கின்ற மனித ெநᾞக்கᾊ- மனித அவலம் என்பைத மறந்ᾐவிடாதீர்கள்!

ெகளரவ ᾐைணச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கேள, நான் அதிக ேநரம் ேபச விᾞம்பவில்ைல. எனக்கு மிகக் குᾠகிய ேநரம்தான் ஒᾐக்கப்பட்ᾊᾞக்கின்றᾐ. நான் ெதாடர்ந்ᾐம் ேபசினால், பதிலளிக்கத் தயாராக இᾞக்கின்ற என்ᾔைடய மதிப்ᾗக்குாிய நண்பர், ெகளரவ ெவளிவிவகார அைமச்சரவர்கᾦைடய ேநரத்ைத நான் எᾌப்பதாக ᾙᾊந்ᾐவிᾌம். எனேவ, மீண்ᾌம் இந்த நாட்ᾌக்கான எதிர்காலம் ஒளிமயமானதாக இᾞக்கப்ேபாகின்றதா அல்லᾐ ெதாடர்ந்ᾐம் இᾞண்ட, இரத்தம் சிந்ᾐகின்ற பிரச்சிைனகளின் நᾌவிேல சிக்கித் தவிக்கின்ற ஒᾞ நாடாகத்தான் இந்த நாᾌ நீᾊத்திᾞக்கப்ேபாகின்றதா என்பைத ேமதகு ஜனாதிபதி அவர்கᾦம் இந்த அரசாங்கத்தினᾞம்தான் தீர்மானிக்கப்ேபாகின்றார்கெளன்பைத அᾨத்தந்திᾞத்தமாகக் கூறி, தமிழ்த் ேதசியக் கூட்டைமப்ᾗ எந்தச் சந்தர்ப்பத்திᾤம், என்ன

1879 1880

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව

* කථාව අවසානෙය් පළ කර ඇත. உைரயினிᾠதியில் தரப்பட்ᾌள்ளᾐ. Produced at end of speech.

[ගරු එන්. ශී කාන්තා මහතා]

விைல ெகாᾌத்ᾐம், தமிழ் மக்கᾦைடய ேதசிய அபிலாைஷகᾦக்காக ஜனநாயக வழியில் ெதாடர்ந்ᾐம் ேபாராᾌம் என்பைத வᾢᾜᾠத்தி என்ᾔைடய ேபச்சிைன ᾙᾊத்ᾐக் ெகாள்கின்ேறன். நன்றி.

ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (විෙද්ශ කටයුතු අමාතɕතුමා)

(மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம - ெவளிநாட்டᾤவல்கள் அைமச்சர்)

(The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama - Minister of Foreign Affairs)

ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, ෙම් අවස්ථාෙව්දී ෙම් සභා ගර්භය තුළ ඉදිරිපත් කර තිෙබන සභාව කල් තැබීෙම් ෙයෝජනාවට රජය ෙවනුෙවන් සම්බන්ධ වන්නට අවස්ථාව ලබා දීම ගැන මම විෙශේෂෙයන්ම ස්තුතිවන්ත වනවා. ගරු විමල් වීරවංශ මන්තීතුමාෙග් ෙයෝජනාව තුළින් අංශ ෙදකක් ගැන අප දැනුවත් වුණා. එක අංශයක් තමයි ෙනෝර්ෙව් පිහිටි ශී ලංකා තානාපති කාර්යාලයට පසු ගිය අවස්ථාවක සිදු වුණු පහර දීම සම්බන්ධෙයන් ෙම් වන විට ෙගන තිෙබන කියා මාර්ග ෙමොනවාද කියන එක. මූලිකවම ඒ සම්බන්ධෙයන් විස්තරයක් මම ෙම් ගරු සභාව හමුෙව් තැබීමට බලාෙපොෙරොත්තු වනවා.

ඉන් අනතුරුව ෙම් අවස්ථාෙව්දී ශී ලංකාෙව් ෙකෙරන මානුෂීය ෙමෙහවර පිළිබඳව ශී ලංකා රජය ෙගන ඇති කියා මාර්ග ගැන ජාතɕන්තර සම්බන්ධතාව අප ෙකොයි විධියට ද ෙම් අවස්ථාෙව්දී ජාතික නɕාය පතයක් තුළ ඒකාබද්ධ කර ගන්ෙන් කියන ෙම් කාරණා පිළිබඳව ෙම් ගරු සභාව දැනුවත් කරන්නට මා බලාෙපොෙරොත්තු වනවා.

ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, මූලික වශෙයන් ෙනෝර්ෙව් පිහිටි ශී ලංකා තානාපති කාර්යාලයට පහර දීම සම්බන්ධෙයන් මෙග් පකාශය ඉංගීසි භාෂාෙවන් ෙම් ගරු සභාව ෙවත ෙයොමු කරන්නට ඔබතුමන්ෙග් අවසරය ඉල්ලා සිටිනවා.

Hon. Deputy Speaker, the Hon. Wimal Weerawansa has raised a matter of national importance and given the significance of the subject matter, I wish to respond to his statement as follows.

Firstly, I will deal with the attack carried out by operatives of the LTTE’s international terror network on our Embassy in Oslo on Sunday, 12th April, 2009. As the Hon. Members would be aware, the Government of Sri Lanka immediately condemned the attack in the strongest possible terms and on the very next day itself, summoned the Royal Norwegian Ambassador in Colombo to the Foreign Ministry and lodged a strong protest at the failure of the Norwegian authorities to take adequate security measures to prevent this premeditated and cowardly assault on our Embassy in Oslo.

As stated in my formal communication to the Norwegian Government, this attack was a clear breach of Norway’s internationally-binding legal obligations to afford protection to diplomatic premises on its territory in terms of the Vienna Convention on Diplomatic Relations of 18th April, 1961. In the immediate aftermath of the incident, the Foreign Ministry also issued a statement denouncing the attack. I wish to table* this media release, which is self-explanatory, to be included in Hansard.

It was in the spirit of statesmanship and humanitarian goodwill that President Mahinda Rajapaksa issued a directive to the armed forces on 12th April, 2009 to restrict their operations to those of a defensive nature in order to give the civilian population held hostage in the No-fire Zone by the LTTE the opportunity to celebrate the Sinhala and Tamil New Year in a suitable atmosphere. However, this festive goodwill gesture of the President was marred by the premeditated attack on our Mission in Norway. As this House is aware, in the recent past there have been a number of demonstrations organized by the LTTE’s international network across the globe.

Hon. Members, this attack displays the contempt with which the LTTE has continued to treat the repeated concessions made by the Sri Lankan Government. In these circumstances, the Norwegian Government was informed that the Government of Sri Lanka perceived that it was no longer feasible for Norway to act as a facilitator in its engagements with Sri Lanka in the current context. We strongly urged the Norwegian Government to apprehend the perpetrators of the attack and bring them to justice.

My Norwegian counterpart, Jonas Gahre Store, immediately condemned the attack on our Mission. In a Statement issued by the Norwegian Foreign Ministry on the day of the incident itself, on 12th April, he stated, “I deeply deplore the fact that unauthorized persons unlawfully forced their way into the Sri Lankan Embassy in Oslo and caused extensive damage. This is a violation of Norwegian law and an action that is totally unacceptable”.

The Deputy Leader of the Opposition Progress Party, Per Sandberg, also denounced the attack. In a statement he said, “When one attacks and vandalizes an Embassy, one is not only in violation of Norwegian law, but one is almost making a declaration of war. I take it for granted that this would be investigated thoroughly and that the people responsible for the destruction are immediately sent out of the country and back to Sri Lanka, no matter what conditions they may face there”.

Within two hours of the incident, Mr. Jon Hanssen Bauer, the Norwegian Special Envoy to Sri Lanka, visited the Embassy and expressed his deepest sympathy to our Ambassador on behalf of the Norwegian Government. The Chief of Protocol of their Foreign Ministry also visited the Embassy to convey the Norwegian Government’s condemnation of the incident. The Minister of International Development, Erik Solheim, who was on vacation at that time, contacted our Ambassador and condemned the attack on our Mission in the strongest possible terms, terming the attack as an “outrage” which was “totally unacceptable”.

Immediately after the attack on the Embassy, the Norwegian Police issued a public apology for failing in their duty to prevent the attack. The Chief Police

1881 1882

2009 මැයි 06

Inspector, Johan Fredriksen stated, “This is something we are sincerely apologetic about. We are humble and very apologetic for what has happened, and it is without a doubt, the Police’s responsibility to maintain security at foreign missions in Oslo”. I wish to inform the Hon. Members that the Norwegian Police had taken in 12 persons. නමුත් අෙප් ගරු මන්තීතුමා කිව්වා එක් ෙකෙනක් පමණයි කියලා. නමුත් ෙම් වන විට ෙදොෙළොස් ෙදෙනක් අත් අඩංගුවට අර ෙගන තිෙබනවා in connection with the terror attack on our Embassy. Further investigations are continuing at two levels, one by the Oslo Police and the other by the Police Security Service - PST - at a higher level. The Head of the Counter Terrorism Department of the Police Security Service, who is closely monitoring the investigations, is in constant touch with our Embassy officials and we expect the Norwegian authorities to prosecute all those involved and mete out stern punishment to the convicted offenders. I have noted a statement released by the Norwegian Government that the Sri Lankan Government would be compensated for the material damage caused to the Mission premises. I thank the Norwegian Government for this gesture, but I wish to state that the Government of Sri Lanka would be undertaking the repairs to the damaged premises at its own cost. We will not seek any compensation or expect repairs to be made by the Norwegian Government. We will be doing our repairs at our own cost accordingly. In response to the terror attack on our Mission in Oslo, the Norwegian authorities have strengthened security measures for both the Embassy and the staff. Round the clock security has now been provided for the Mission premises too - police officers and police vehicles have been deployed in the vicinity of the Embassy. A security cover has also been provided for the Mission staff. I wish to emphasize that the traditional warm and friendly relations that Sri Lanka enjoys with Norway have not been in any manner undermined on account of this unfortunate incident. There was much loose talk of our downgrading diplomatic relations with Norway. That is far from it. Our relationship with Norway is one of endurance and goodwill. Following the return of our previous Ambassador in Oslo, Mr. Rodney Perera, a senior officer of the Sri Lanka Foreign Service has already taken up his post as Ambassador Designate and will be shortly presenting his credentials to the Norwegian monarch. On the positive side, the average Norwegian citizen’s perspective of Sri Lanka, heavily influenced by the pro-LTTE propaganda, has also undergone a dramatic change following the attack on our Embassy, the footage of which was shown on television. I believe we can now look forward to a better understanding and appreciation of the real situation in our country by the Norwegian Government and the people.

Sir, I made a formal statement in terms of how we have reacted to the attack on our Mission in Oslo. Now, there is a bigger picture that we have to deal with. ගරු ලක්ෂ්මන් කිරිඇල්ල මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு லῆமன் கிாிஎல்ல) (The Hon. Lakshman Kiriella) ගරු ඇමතිතුමනි, ඔබතුමාෙග් අවසරය ඇතිව මම ෙම්ක කියනවා. "එළවන්න කලින් යන්න" කියලා අගමැතිතුමා ෙනෝර්ෙව් රටට කියූ පකාශයක් "ලක්බිම" පත්තරෙය් තිෙබනවා මම දැක්කා. ඒ ගැන මම ඔබතුමාෙගන් අහන්න කැමැතියි.

ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) I think it will be better answered by the Hon. Prime Minister if you raise that when he is here in the House.

ගරු ලක්ෂ්මන් කිරිඇල්ල මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு லῆமன் கிாிஎல்ல) (The Hon. Lakshman Kiriella) "එළවන්න කලින් යන්න" කියලා අගමැතිතුමා ෙනෝර්ෙව් රටට කිව්වාය කියා "ලක්බිම" පත්තරෙය් තිබුණා.

ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) මෙග් මිත ගරු මන්තීතුමනි, මෙග් කාලය. ගරු අගමැතිතුමා ෙම් සභාෙව් ඉන්න ෙවලාවක ඔබතුමා ඒක අහන්න. විෙශේෂෙයන්ම රෙට් ස්ථාවරය මම පැහැදිලි කළ යුතුයි. විෙද්ශ පතිපත්තිය විධියට අප ඉතාමත්ම සමීපව - I think for the first time we are countering terrorism in its full measure and in a comprehensive manner that today we are encountering the world at large, the international community with an equal commitment and wider engagement. That is the most salient feature of President Mahinda Rajapaksa’s foreign relations. How we administer this Government’s foreign relations lies in the test of it, how we deal with each situation. Nowhere in the history of Sri Lanka have we ever taken on the LTTE in the manner in which we have taken it on today. In order to do that, we had the total support and commitment of the entire international community, which I am proud to state here as the Foreign Minister of Sri Lanka.

After the visit of the Right Honourable David Miliband, the Foreign Secretary of Great Britain, what did he have to say about the LTTE? I will now quote from his statement in the House of Commons immediately after returning from his visit to Sri Lanka. Now, Sir, may I quote the Foreign Secretary of the United Kingdom, the Right Honourable David Miliband.

“We emphasized that if the LTTE had any heart at all, it would let the civilians leave the conflict zone.”

It is the LTTE that is preventing people from leaving the conflict zone. I also had the benefit of meeting with the United Kingdom’s Parliamentary Delegation that visited us yesterday and in that, there were five Members who visited the camps in Vavuniya. They include, Desmond Henry Browne, Malcolm Gray Bruce, Edward McGrady, Mohammad Sarwar and also John Simon Bercow. These Members met me that evening.

1883 1884

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව

ගරු ලක්ෂ්මන් කිරිඇල්ල මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு லῆமன் கிாிஎல்ல) (The Hon. Lakshman Kiriella) Sir, I rise to a point of Order. ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) Hon. Member, I did not disturb you. I have very limited time.

නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමා (பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள்) (The Deputy Speaker) There is a point of Order. ගරු කිරිඇල්ල මන්තීතුමාට mike එක ෙදන්න.

ගරු ලක්ෂ්මන් කිරිඇල්ල මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு லῆமன் கிாிஎல்ல) (The Hon. Lakshman Kiriella) එතුමා ෙගනා ෙයෝජනාෙව් තිෙබන්ෙන් ජාතɕන්තර පජාව; සමහර රටවල් අෙප් රටට අනවශɕ විධියට මැදිහත් ෙවනවාය කියලායි. මා ගරු විෙද්ශ කටයුතු ඇමතිතුමාෙගන් අහන්නට කැමතියි, ඒ රටවල් ෙමොනවා ද කියා.

ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) තමුන්නාන්ෙසේ මට ෙම් කථාව කරන්නට ෙදන්ෙන් නැහැ ෙන. මා කථාව කර ෙගන යන ෙකොට you are raising a point of Order.

ගරු ලක්ෂ්මන් කිරිඇල්ල මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு லῆமன் கிாிஎல்ல) (The Hon. Lakshman Kiriella) ෙම්කට අදාළව කථා කරන්න. මම අහන්න කැමැතියි, ඒ රටවල් ෙමොනවා ද කියා.

ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) Now, let me get on to the point. නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමා (பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள்) (The Deputy Speaker) ගරු ඇමතිතුමා කථා කරන්න. ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) What did these people have to say? Two matters got developed here. I am not saying that anyone is interfering with Sri Lanka.

එකම රටකින්වත් ශී ලංකාෙව් ස්වාධිපතɕයටවත්, ශී ලංකා රජය තස්තවාදය මර්දනය කරන්නට ෙම් ෙගන යන කියාදාමයටවත් කිසිම අත ෙපවීමක් ඇත්ෙත්ත් නැහැ, අත ෙපවීමකට ඉඩක් තබන්ෙන්ත් නැහැ කියන එක මා ඉතාමත්ම පැහැදිලිව පකාශ කරනවා.

ගරු ලක්ෂ්මන් කිරිඇල්ල මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு லῆமன் கிாிஎல்ல) (The Hon. Lakshman Kiriella) විමල් වීරවංශ මන්තීතුමා කියන්ෙන් ෙවනත් කථාවක්. ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) ඉතින් මට කථා කරන්න ෙදන්ෙන් නැහැ ෙන්. රජය ෙවනුෙවන් මා කථා කරන්ෙන්.

නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමා (பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள்) (The Deputy Speaker) ගරු ඇමතිතුමා කථා කරන්න. ඔබතුමාට තව විනාඩි පහයි තිෙබන්ෙන්. [බාධා කිරීමක්]

ගරු ලක්ෂ්මන් කිරිඇල්ල මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு லῆமன் கிாிஎல்ல) (The Hon. Lakshman Kiriella) Sir, I rise to a point of Order. ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) ඇයි තමුන්නාන්ෙසේලා ෙම්කට අකැමැතිද? ජාතɕන්තර අත ෙපවීමක් නැති වීම ගැන තමුන්නාන්ෙසේලා අකැමැතිද?

ගරු ලක්ෂ්මන් කිරිඇල්ල මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு லῆமன் கிாிஎல்ல) (The Hon. Lakshman Kiriella) ඔබතුමා ෙම් විවාදයට අනුකූලව, - [බාධා කිරීමක්] ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) නැහැ. මෙග් අනුකූලතාව,-[බාධා කිරීමක්] නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමා (பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள்) (The Deputy Speaker) මන්තීතුමාත් අනුකූලව කථා කෙළේ නැහැ ෙන්. ගරු ඇමතිතුමා කථාව අවසාන කරන්න. [බාධා කිරීමක්]

ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) This is my response. ගරු ලක්ෂ්මන් කිරිඇල්ල මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு லῆமன் கிாிஎல்ல) (The Hon. Lakshman Kiriella) ඔබතුමා කියනවා කිසිම රටකින් හිරිහැරයක් නැහැ කියා. විමල් වීරවංශ මන්තීතුමා කියනවා තිෙබනවා කියා.

ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) ඉතින් ඒක එතුමාෙග් මතය. නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමා (பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள்) (The Deputy Speaker) ගරු ඇමතිතුමා කරුණාකර කථාව අවසන් කරන්න.

1885 1886

2009 මැයි 06

ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) ගරු මන්තීතුමනි, තමුන්නාන්ෙසේ ඊර්ෂɕා ද? ජාතɕන්තර පජාවෙග් අත ෙපවීමක් නැති වීම ගැන ඊර්ෂɕා ද? ජාතɕන්තර පජාවෙග් අත ෙපවීමක් තිබුණත් ඒ අත ෙපවීමට යටත් ෙනොවන එක ගැනත් ඊර්ෂɕා ද? මහින්ද රාජපක්ෂ රජෙය් පතිපත්තිය ෙමන්න ෙම්කයි. අප ෙද්ශීය නɕාය පතයක් අනුවයි ෙම් වැඩ පිළිෙවළ කියාවට නඟන්ෙන්.

විෙශේෂෙයන්ම ගරු එන්. ශී කාන්තා මන්තීතුමාටත් මට උත්තර ෙදන්නට තිෙබනවා. එතුමාත් ෙම් පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව තුළ වැදගත් පකාශයක් කළා. එතුමා කියනවා, අද අවශɕතාව තිෙබන්ෙන්, ෙම්කට ෙද්ශපාලන විසඳුමක් කරා එක්කාසු වී යන කමෙව්දයක් අප ෙගොඩ නඟා ගැනීමයි කියන එක. That is the way forward. No one has said there is no political solution that lies ahead of us. We are committed towards a political solution.

Let me explain in this House the issue that is before us today. To the question whether international pressure is mounting and whether we are going to subscribe to the international pressure, the answer is "no". We have a local agenda that we are pursuing right across the globe and the world community is being educated well enough to understand the gravity of the situation in Sri Lanka and to be supportive of the Government’s agenda currently being pursued. ෙමන්න ෙම් වචන ටික මෙගන් කියවා ගන්න මට බාධා කරන්ෙන් නැතිව හිටියා නම් මීට වඩා ෙලෙහසි වනවා.

ඒ ෙකෙසේ ෙවතත්, විෙශේෂෙයන් I have to respond to this matter. Yes, our President went to the United Kingdom. At that time, what were we looking at? We were even going to Geneva; we were even talking at that time to the LTTE to come to a negotiated settlement. That is what our President expected by going to the United Kingdom, meeting with Tony Blair, who was the Prime Minister at that time, discussing their own experiences in the North Ireland issue and experimenting how best we could address these matters outside a military engagement. But, all those things did not succeed and that is why we were compelled, with the development in Mavil Aru when they closed the Mavil Aru anicut that was supplying water to the Eastern Province, to engage militarily and succeed in clearing the entire Eastern Province. Now, we want to replicate our success in the Northern Province with the humanitarian mission we have undertaken today in freeing the people from the clutches of the LTTE. That is our mission. That mission is being witnessed by the international community and we welcome their presence, their assistance and understanding as to how we are attending to this difficult task. That is the issue before us.

I would like as much as my Colleague - the Hon. Wimal Weerawansa called upon the Opposition to join hands in addressing this issue - for us to say in one voice to the outside world that the issue lies here. Let us join hands and explain to the world at large how the Government is looking at this matter. What was the reaction coming from my learned Friend from the United National Party? My good Friend straight off started saying that the issue is on the domestic agenda, the issue

is in the domestic polity. That is what we must avoid when we address the fundamental, core issues that are affecting a nation. We would like a wider understanding to prevail when we get our message across to the international community.

Having said that, today I am happy that we could look at the challenges before us. What are the challenges that are before us? The first is, how to get the balance civilians who are entrapped by the LTTE and kept as hostages in the No-fire Zone, which is now restricted to about four and a half square kilometres, out. The second issue is the welfare of the civilians, numbering 120,000, who have fled the No-fire Zone within a period of less than 72 hours, escaping the hold of the LTTE, facing the threats coming from the LTTE and resisting the bullets fired or directed at them. They were waiting to be freed by the Government and they came over to the cleared areas embracing the military as the protectors of the civilian population who were entrapped by the LTTE. They preferred the military over the LTTE. They preferred not only the Government, but also the military apparatus of the Government as protectors of the Tamil civilians who were entrapped by the LTTE.

The next challenge that lies ahead of us is, how we are going to treat the IDPs. - [Interruption.] Yes, my Friend? - [Interruption.] No, no. I have all the time for my Friend.

නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමා (பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள்) (The Deputy Speaker) ගරු ඇමතිතුමා, ඔබතුමා කථාව අවසන් කරන්න. ගරු එන්. ශී කාන්තා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு என். ᾯ காந்தா) (The Hon. N. Sri Kantha)

Our grievance is this. The Government cannot gain the remaining territory without causing deaths to thousands of civilians who are trapped there.

ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) My Friend, you and I have always shared this issue. You never expected 120,000 civilians to flee within 48 hours. Was it your own conviction that it would have been possible at that time? Your answer would have been "no" if we had raised this issue, may be a month ago. - [Interruption.] But today, with regard to the balance, the remaining civilians, success has been shown in our engagement. We will succeed. We will succeed with greater responsibility. We will not have any collateral damage coming on to the civilians and we will engage ourselves in the most careful, the most responsible and the most accountable manner when dealing with the balance civilians who are trapped by the LTTE. No longer can we also tolerate the entrapment of civilians by the LTTE terrorist organization. [Interruption.] I could not finish -

1887 1888

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව

ගරු එන්. ශී කාන්තා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு என். ᾯ காந்தா) (The Hon. N. Sri Kantha) Our accusation is this. You are crushing the Tamil civilians. Why do you say that you are trying to free them from the clutches of the LTTE? - [Interruption.]

ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) Yes, we are doing that. - [Interruption.] We are not killing the Tamil civilians. You must go to the camps there. Now, listen to this. If you came and discussed with the President yesterday, in response to his invitation that was extended to the TNA to come over, sit and discuss with him the matter that affects your people, our people - the people of Sri Lanka - we could address these matters in a better way and in a more pragmatic and a practical way.

ගරු එන්. ශී කාන්තා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு என். ᾯ காந்தா) (The Hon. N. Sri Kantha) If the military operations could be halted, we are ready to meet the President now.-[Interruption.]

ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) Do not throw a lifeline to the LTTE. - [Interruption.] Let the LTTE die. Let the civilians live. Let the LTTE die. Let the civilians live.

ගරු එන්. ශී කාන්තා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு என். ᾯ காந்தா) (The Hon. N. Sri Kantha) My good Friend, Mr. Anandasangaree, who is also your good friend, has stated that there are more than one lakh of civilians - [Interruption.]

ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) Fair enough. Let there be even more. But, we are responsible for each one of them. Statistics will not count. What matters is every single life. That is what matters to the Government of Sri Lanka. You all are going by numbers. What are the numbers with regard to the LTTE, if this is a case of numbers? The LTTE, as a terrorist organization, has to be dealt with the manner in which they deserve to be dealt with. Civilians have to be protected and that is our responsibility as the Government of Sri Lanka. That is why we are getting more and more engaged. What did the civilians have to say to the British Members of Parliament whose names I just quoted, the five of them? The list is here. They said that the LTTE was preventing them from coming and were shooting at them when they attempted to come and that is the

behaviour of the LTTE - shooting their own people; our people; the Sri Lankans - the Tamil community. This is the treatment that the LTTE was giving them.

Now, the international community has come here to witness this. That is why I am happy that my good Friend, the Hon. Lakshman Kiriella asked whether we are ready to deal with the international community. The answer is, “Yes.” We are dealing with them in an integrated manner, in a wider manner, in a more penetrating manner and that is why you will see more visitors coming at my invitation to Sri Lanka, such as ministers of foreign affairs, with whom we could engage in discussions and who in turn will go back and speak in their countries to the Tamil diaspora and to the Sri Lankan community and thereby will educate the people on what is right, what is wrong and what is happening in Sri Lanka. In fact, having visited the IDP camps in Vavuniya, one of the members said that he should be at the Trafalgar Square. Why should he be at the Trafalgar Square? That is to tell back to the LTTE demonstrators that this is the true situation in Sri Lanka. I must compliment the Hon. Member who stated that to me yesterday and I am sure that he will demonstrate his commitment by us. When the Minister of International Cooperation, Mrs. B. J. Oda came from Canada at my invitation, what did she find? She found a very extensive arrangement being made to take care of the IDPs in Sri Lanka. Where else have you seen this type of a sudden IDP development taking place being addressed by any authority or any government? Nowhere in the world! These visitors who come to Sri Lanka have seen other locations in the world. That is why I am quite happy and confident that we will address this issue well. As much as my learned Friend, the Hon. N. Sri Kantha has said, let us engage in a dialogue to see where the political process would take us in the future. Let us get the LTTE out of our way. Let it have its death as a terrorist organization. Let the people live in Sri Lanka as a country where all of us can be part of it and I must compliment the Hon. Wimal Weerawansa for giving me the opportunity to bring this up.

එක්සත් ජාතීන්ෙග් සංවිධානය ඇතුළු ජාතɕන්තර සංවිධාන සහ ජාතɕන්තර පජාව සමඟ ෙම් අවස්ථාෙව්දී අප කර ෙගන යන කියාදාමය සම්බන්ධෙයන් පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුවට පැහැදිලි පකාශයක් කිරීමට ෙම් වාෙග් අවස්ථාවක් ලබා දීම ගැන මා එතුමාට ස්තුතිවන්ත වනවා. විෙශේෂෙයන්ම අද මානුෂීය ෙමෙහයුම සඳහා ජාතɕන්තර පජාව ෙගන් ලැෙබන සහෙයෝගය අර ෙගන, ඔවුන්ෙග් අදහස් අපෙග් අදහස් සමඟ සන්සන්දනය කර ෙගන, ශී ලංකාවට ආෙව්ණික, ජාතික පශ්නයක් වන තස්තවාදය පරාජය කිරීෙම් අවශɕතාව හඳුනා ෙගන එය ශී ලංකා ජාතික නɕාය පතයක් තුළ විසඳා ගන්න අපි උත්සාහ කරන්න ඕනෑ. ඒ අනුව කටයුතු කිරීෙම් අවකාශය ඉදිරිෙය්දී එන්න එන්නම වැඩි ෙවමින් තිෙබනවා. අන්න ඒකයි අපි ලබා තිෙබන සුවිෙශේෂ ජයගහණය.

ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, මට ෙම් අවස්ථාව ලබා දීම ගැන මා ඔබතුමාට ස්තුතිවන්ත වනවා. ඒ වාෙග්ම විපක්ෂෙයන් කථා කළ ගරු මන්තීතුමන්ලා ෙදපළටම විෙශේෂෙයන්ම මා මිත ලක්ෂ්මන් කිරිඇල්ල මැතිතුමාටත්, මා මිත ශීකාන්තා මැතිතුමාටත් ස්තුතිවන්ත වනවා. ඒ වාෙග්ම ෙම් ෙයෝජනාව ෙගනාපු අපෙග් විමල් වීරවංශ මැතිතුමාටත් ස්තුතිවන්ත වනවා, රජය ෙවනුෙවන් මට ෙම් අවස්ථාව ලබා දීම ගැන.

විෙද්ශ කටයුතු අමාතɕාංශය ெவளிநாட்ᾌ அᾤவல்கள் அைமச்சு

MINISTRY OF FOREIGN AFFAIRS ‘குᾊயரசுக் கட்ᾊடம்’, ெகாᾨம்ᾗ 1, இலங்ைக මෙග් අංකය ඔෙබ් අංකය දිනය எனᾐ இல. உமᾐ இல. திகதி My No. Your No. Date

MEDIA RELEASE GOVERNMENT CONDEMNS TERROR ATTACK ON

SRI LANKA MISSION IN OSLO The Government of Sri Lanka vehemently condemns the violent attack by operatives belonging to the international terror network of the LTTE on the Sri Lanka Embassy in Oslo on Sunday, 12 April 2009.

On the advice of the Minister of Foreign Affairs, Rohitha Bogollagama, the Royal Norwegian Ambassador in Sri Lanka, Tore Hattrem was summoned to the Foreign Ministry today (13th April 2009), and an official protest lodged. The following matters were brought to the attention of the Ambassador in connection with the attack on the Sri Lankan mission in the Norwegian capital yesterday.

* The Sri Lanka Government strongly condemns the premeditated

attack on the Sri Lanka Embassy in Oslo on Sunday, 12th April 2009 by operatives of the international terror network of the LTTE. * In the recent past, there have been a number of demonstrations

organized by the LTTE’s international network across the globe. On this particular day (12th April) too, a demonstration was held with the permission of the Norwegian Government. The said attack was subsequent to this demonstration. * The Norwegian Government, being fully cognizant of the modus

operandi of the LTTE and in constant contact with its international network as well as its leadership in the North of Sri Lanka, ought to have ensured the provision of adequate security to the diplomatic premises and agents of the Sri Lanka Government as obligated by the Vienna Convention on Diplomatic Relations of 18th April 1961. Article 22(2) of the Convention casts a special duty on the receiving State “to take all appropriate steps to protect the premises of the mission against any intrusion or damage and to prevent any disturbance of the peace of the mission or impairment of its dignity.” * Furthermore, requests for adequate security for the Mission had

been made repeatedly by the Ambassador of Sri Lanka to Norway, who had been informed by the authorities that since the Norwegian Security Service was maintaining a constant surveillance of the Mission, they did not perceive the necessary to place a static guard to provide security cover. * In this context, the Government of Sri Lanka deplores the failure

of the Norwegian Government in fulfilling its obligations under international law, consequent to its sheer neglect in the provision of adequate security to the Sri Lanka Mission in Oslo. * Quite in contrast, the Government of Sri Lanka has been

continuously providing security to Norway’s diplomatic representation in Sri Lanka at all times, notwithstanding the constraints of manpower and other resources on the Police and security agencies.

* It was fortunate that none of the staff of the Sri Lanka Embassy

came to harm due to their absence from the diplomatic premises, when this vicious and violent attack on the Mission took place. * It is deplorable that this act of terror took place within hours of

the presidential directive to the armed forces to restrict their operations to those of a defensive nature, in order to give the civilian population entrapped as hostages by the LTTE, the opportunity to celebrate the Sinhala & Tamil New Year in a suitable atmosphere and have uninhibited freedom of movement from the No Fire Zone to the cleared areas. * This outrageous act of terror committed by the LTTE in Oslo, the

capital of Norway which they feel is a location due the moral backing available locally, should demonstrate to the Norwegian Government, the true character of the LTTE. * Further, is displays that repeated concessions made by the Sri

Lanka Government have been treated only with contempt by the LTTE. * In these circumstances, the Government of Sri Lanka perceives

that it is no longer feasible for Norway to act as facilitator in its engagement with Sri Lanka in the current context. * The Government of Sri Lanka strongly urges the Norwegian

Government to apprehend the perpetrators of the attack on its Embassy in Oslo and bring them to justice immediately. In addition, the Government of Sri Lanka also expects the Norwegian authorities to act swiftly to provide adequate security for the Sri Lanka Mission, as well as all for the staff of the Mission, in keeping with Norway’s international obligations under the Vienna Convention on Diplomatic Relations, and also ensure that there is no recurrence of such incidents in the future.

The violent conduct of LTTE elements conducting various demonstrations elsewhere abroad, amounting to glorification of terrorism, should at least now convince the international community of the absolute intransigence of the LTTE and its callous disregard for international law and civilized norms of behavior.

Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Colombo. 13th April

திᾞத்தப்படாத பிரதி கிைடத்த இᾞ வாரங்கᾦள் ஹன்சாட் பதிப்பாசிாியᾞக்கு அᾔப்ᾗதல் ேவண்ᾌம்.

ෙමම වාර්තාෙව් අවසාන මුදණය සදහා ස්වකීය නිවැරදි කළ යුතු තැන් දක්වනු රිසි මන්තීන් මින් පිටපතක් ෙගන නිවැරදි කළ යුතු ආකාරය එහි පැහැදිලිව ලකුණු ෙකොට, පිටපත ලැබී ෙදසතියක් ෙනොඉක්මවා හැන්සාඩ් සංස්කාරක ෙවත ලැෙබන ෙසේ එවිය යුතුය.

රජෙය් පකාශන කාර්යාංශෙය් අධිකාරී ෙවත සෑම වර්ෂයකම ෙනොවැම්බර් 30දා ට පථම

Subscriptions : The annual subscription for Official Report of Hansard is Rs. 2,178. A single copy of Hansard is available for

Rs. 18.15. (Postage Rs. 2.50) Copies can be obtained by remitting in advance an annual subscription fee to the

SUPERINTENDENT, GOVERNMENT PUBLICATIONS BUREAU, No. 132, Maya Avenue,

Kirulapone, Colombo 5. The fee should reach him on or before November 30 each year .

Late applications for subscriptions will not be accepted.

ශී ලංකා රජෙය් මුදණ ෙදපාර්තෙම්න්තුෙව් මුදණය කරන ලදී.
